BO STAN GCIG PA'I BSTI GNAS NYANG STOD SPOS KHANG GI KUN DGA' RA
BAR BSNYEN PAR RDZOGS PA'I TSE SNGAR DGE CHUL GNANG BA'I MTSAN
GYI STENG DU MKHAN PO'I MTSAN SGRA GRAGS PA RGYAL

@053B MTSAN DPAL BZANG PO ZHES BSNAN ZHING BAG YOD PA KHO NA
MDZAD DE TSUL KHRIMS RNAM PAR DAG BA NI, JI SKAD DU, KHAN MA THO
PHRA RAB LA'ANG, ,THUGS NI SHIN TU 'JIGS PAR MDZAD, ,DRAN DANG
SHES BZHIN LDAN PA YIS, ,CHUL BZHIN MA

YIN YID MI MDZAD, ,BAG YONG DRAN DANG G-YO SGYU MED, ,LTUNG BA'I
NYES PAS KHYOD MA GOS, ,ZHES MNYAM MED JO BO CHEN PO'I RNAM PAR
THAR PA DANG MCHUNGS SA, BZLAS BRJOD NUS PA'I GLAG ZHAGS THOD
'PHRENG LA, ,'KHYUG TSE BDUD SNYING

SNGAGS SMYON THOG GZER GYIS, ,'BIGS KYANG LHA RGYUD BSKUL BA'I
DBYAR GYI RNGA, ,THOS PAS DNGOS GRUB RMA BYA'I MNGAL KHUR 'DZIN,
,BDE STONG YE SHES ME LCES GNYIS 'DZIN SHING, ,BSREG PA'I TSA
'PHRUL LA MTSAR BYIS PA'I BLO, ,SKYON MED GNYUG

MA'I LAM GYIS 'DUS MTHA'I 'PHRANG, ,BRGAL TE BCU GSUM SA LA SNYEG
'DI CI, ,MTHA' KLAS CHOS KYI RANG MTSANG RJEN PA RU, ,SHAR TSE
KUN RDZOB 'KHRUL BA DBYIG PO CHES, ,MED KYANG MNGON SUM SNANG
BA'I SPRUL BSGYUR GYIS, ,SGYU MA'I GLANG SENG

'JIGS CHUL BAG LA ZHA, ,BDAG 'DRA'I 'GRO SNYING LCAGS KHAMS 'KHOR
BA LA, ,NGES PAR MA 'BYUNG TSE 'DI'I GRABS GSHOM NA, ,MTHON PO'I
SA LA GSHEGS KYANG CHANGS SBYONG GRUS, ,SROD MTSOR SGROL BRDZU'I
RJUN GYIS 'DRID 'DI CI, ,'ON

TE CHAGS BRAL TSUL KHRIMS NGAD 'THUL YANG, ,DGA' BZHI'I 'GROS KYI
BDE STONG SMIN LEGS MAR, ,MNYAM SBYOR RTZE DGA' RGOD PA'I THEG
GSUM DON, ,'GAL MED MDUD PA'I GNAD DE LHOD POR GROL, ,GSOL 'DEBS
LAS, ,GRUB DBANG

@054A *, ,BLA MA 'KHOR LO SDOM PAR GZIGS, ,DGE 'PHEL CHOS KYI
KHRI LA SPYAN 'DREN PA'I, ,GZHI BDAG GUS PA'I RNAM 'PHRUL PHO
NYA'I CHUL, ,ZHABS KYI PADMAR SON LA GSOL BA 'DEBS, ,NGAG DBANG
DBYANGS CAN LHA

MO'I BZLAS BRJOD TSE, ,MKHA' LA ME TOG DKAR PO'I CHAR BABS SHANG,
,RGYUD MANGS SGRA SNYAN RNA BA' BDUD RTZI MCHOG ,'OD GSAL DANG DU
GSAN LA GSOL BA 'DEBS, ,MNAL LAM JANG DU DPA' BO MKHA' 'GRO'I
TSOGS, ,SGRON MA

BTEG NAS RJE BTZUN RDO RING PA'I, ,'KHOR SLOB 'CHOL BA'I ZOL GYI
RNAM THAR MCHOG ,RTZOM PAR BSKUL BA GZIGS LA GSOL BA 'DEBS,
,GRANGS MED MKHA' 'GRO 'DU BA'I TSOGS DBUS KYI, ,GTZO MO PADMA'I
DRA BA CAN ZHES PAS, ,

GLEGS BAM BSTAN CING CHO 'PHRUL SNA TSOGS BCAS, ,'DRI BA'I YO
BYAD GTAD LA GSOL BA 'DEBS, ,CHES KYI KHRI LA 'KHOD PA'I RAB
BYUNG GIS, ,RGYAL BA'I RTOGS BRJOD KLOG PA'I TSUL CAN LA, ,MKHA'
'GRO'I TSOGS RNAMS DGA' BAS

NYAN PA SOGS, ,DGE MTSAN DU MA GZIGS LA GSOL BA 'DEBS, ,RJE BTZUN
BLA MAS ZHAL BZANG YANG YANG BSTAN, ,RNAM THAR RTZOM PA'I BYA BA
MTHAR PHYIN TSE, ,DPAL LDAN 'DOD KHAMS DBANG MOS DGYES PA YI,
,SRUNG MAR ZHAL GYIS

BZHES LA GSOL BA 'DEBS, ,ZHES DNGOS SHUGS SNA TSOGS PA, DE LTAR
MKHAS BTZUN BZANG PO'I BDAG NYID CAN RNAMS NI 'KHOR BA'I MTHA' MA
RDZOGS PA DE SRID DU RNAM PAR DKAR BA'I 'PHRIN LAS KYI RGYUN CHAD
PA MED PAR 'JUG PA CHOS NYID

@054B YIN PAS MDO SNGAGS KYI GRA DANG SDE, SA SKYONG BA'I CHE
DGU, RIGS RUS KYIS MTHO BA'I YA RABS, RNAM DPYOD DANG LDAN PA'I
MKHAS PA, NYAMS RTOGS DANG LDAN PA'I SGOM CHEN, DPA' MDZANGS
LONGS SPYOD DANG LDAN PA'I DPON SKYA SOGS SKYA BO

THAMS CAD KYI BSAM BLO'I YUL DU DAM PA 'DI NYID BDAG CAG GI
SKYABS GNAS SU THAB NA CI MA RUNG SNYAM PA'I 'DUN PA RTZE GCIG TU
GYUR PAS, RJE NYID KYIS CHOS SKYONG RNAMS LA BKA' BSGO BA'I TSIGS
BCAD LAS, 'DI NA SKYE RGU'I PHAN BDE MA LUS PA,

RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA MCHOG LA RAG LAS SHING, ,BYANG PHYOGS 'DI NA
BSTAN PA'I SNYING PO MCHOG ,SA SKYA'I RJE BTZUN ZHABS LAS BRGYUD
'DI YIN, ,DE YI YANG SNYING GSANG CHEN ZAB MO'I BCUD, ,ZHAL DANG
SNYAN DU BRGYUD PA'I MDZOD 'DZIN PA, ,KHO

BO'I 'DREN MCHOG RJE BTZUN RDO RING ZHABS, ,BKA' DRIN MNYAM MED
DAM PA'I SROL 'DIR BAS, ,DE NYID MCHOD CING BKUR BA'I SBYIN PA'I
BDAG ,STOD LUNG SA YI THIG LE'I STOBS LDAN NI, ,SPA RA BA ZHES
GRAGS PA'I BA DAN CAN, ,ZHES PA LTAR

STOD LUNG NAS SDE BA SPA RA BA RJE BTZUN SA SKYA BA'I BSTAN PA LA
MI PHYED PA'I DAD PA DANG LDAN PAS GSUNG NGAG RIN PO CHE'I BLA MA
BRGYUD PA'I GSER SKU GRVA TSAR BZHENGS PA'I RAB GNAS LA GDAN
DRANGS TE STOD NAS CHIBS KHA BSKYOD, DAM TSIG PA

LA YE SHES SEMS DPA' DNGOS SU 'JUG PAS MTSON 'DOD CHOS RKYEN SEL
GYI RIM GRO SOGS RA BA YONGS SU SKONG BAR MDZAD CING, RDO RJE'I
CHOS SKYONG RNAMS KYI RTAG GTOR 'DZUGS PA SOGS MGON KHANG BZHENG
BA GNANG TSE, NA MO GU RU DE WA

@055A *, ,MAndA LA DHARMA P'A LA SA PA RI W'A RE BHYA: KUN KHYAB
KUN GYI BYED PO GCIG NYID SRID ZHI'I GZUGS KYIS KUN LA 'KHYUD,
,RGYAL DANG RGYAL SRAS SLOB MAR BCAS BA'I TSOGS KYI GTZO BO RGYAL
BA RJE, ,MTHA' YAS MTHA' MED 'GRO

BA'I SKYABS MCHOG RJE BTZUN BLA MA SRID MTHA' BAR, ,GTZUG RGYAN
GTZUG GI NOR BUR GUS MCHOD 'BRAL BA MED PAR GTZUG TU BZHUGS,
,ZHES SOGS MKHA' 'GRO LNGA BSTOD BSKUL DANG, DAM CAN SRUNG MA
DGYES PA'I RNAL 'BYOR PA, ,RDO RJE 'DZIN

PA BLO GSAL RGYA MTSO'I SDES, ,GNAS LUGS BDE BA CHEN PO'I MKHA'
DBYINGS SU, RAB ZAB THABS KYIS BSGRUBS PA'I MCHOD PA'I SPRIN,
,ZHES RGYUD DANG MAN NGAG LAS BYUNG BA'I PHYI NANG GSANG MCHOD
RGYAS PAR DBUL MTHAR, RGYAL BA'I BSTAN

PA SPYI DANG BYE BRAG TU, ,DPAL LDAN SA SKYA PA ZHES GRAGS PA YI,
,BSTAN PA'I NYING KHU RJE BTZUN RDO RING BA'I, ,BSTAN PAS YI
PHYOGS 'DIR DAR RGYAS MDZOD, ,DE NYID 'DZIN DANG MCHOD PA'I SBYIN
PA'I BDAG ,MI NOR 'KHOR BCAS BSRUNG DANG

SPA BA DANG, ,'DU 'BRAL MED PAR RTAG TU SKYONG BAR MDZOD, ,CES
DANG, DA LTA'I GNOD BYED MI DANG MI MA YIN, ,SKAD CIG NYID LA
MNGON SUM 'DIR KHUG LA, ,RAB RNON MTSON CHAS MGO LUS DUM BUR
GTUBS, ,KHRAG ZHAG DON SNYING DMAR

PO HAB KYIS THOB, ,CES 'BRIN LAS RGYAS PAR MDZAD, RING ZHIG NA
'GRO BA'I LAS SMIN BDO BA RGYAL PO GZUGS CAN SNYING PO LTAR TSAD
BZUNG DKA' MOD, HOR BYA RIG SOGS RJES MA RNAMS LA'ANG SRUNG MA'I
ZA KHA ZUG STE MING GI LHAG MAR GYUR,

@055B DBUS SU ZLA BA DRUG TZAM GYI RING BSTAN 'GRO'I LEGS TSOGS
SPEL NAS GTZANG DU BYON, CHOS SGO BA BYAMS PA SHES RAB BZANG PO
LA SNGAR SMOS PA'I CHOS GSAN RGYU'I SNGON DU RMU GSHOD NA BZHUGS
PA'I MNAL LAM DU MI SNGON PO ZHIG NA RE PHUN 'KHOR

DGE 'PHEL GYI ZHAL BDAG MDZAD DGOS

ZHIG BABS BYUNG NAS GUS PA CHEN POS PHYAG BTZAL TE THUB BSTAN DGE
'PHEL GYI GDAN SA LA SPYAN 'DREN PAR

YONGS PA YIN ZER BA LA KHYED SU YIN GSUNGS PAS, BDAG SHO DMAR GYI

DU DRAG SHUL DANG GDUG RTZUB CHE BAS THUB BSTAN DGE 'PHEL GYI 'OG

RKANG 'GROS BYAD, PHYAG RDZOGS KYI

@056B BA'I DPAL LA BKOD, DE NAS MI RING BAR KHA CHE 'DUS BZANG
MKHAS MCHOG DA BYIG GNYEN GYI PHYOGS SU BYON BA BZHIN DUR SMRIG
GOS KYI NAM MKHA'I KHA DOG 'GYUR BA LTA BU'I 'DUS TSOGS KYI SER
SBRENG 'PHAN GDUGS RGYAL MTSAN ROL CHA SOGS MCHOD

TSOGS BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PA THOGS PAS MDUN BDAR CHIBS BSU'I BKOD
PA SNGON DU 'GRO BAS RGYAL BA ZHES PA SHING PHO RTA'I LO THUB
BSTAN DGE 'PHEL GYI GDAN SENG GE'I KHRI LA ZHABS KYI CHU SKYES
RNAM PAR BKOD, DE NAS KHAMS BA SANGS RGYAS RDO

RJE, MI NYAG MGON PO 'OD ZER, CHOS RJE BRAG CHOS PA, PHU PA DBU
MDZAD TSUL KHRIMS SOGS RIN PO CHE LTA BU'I GDUL BYA DBANG PO YANG

BSHAD, GZHAN YANG DBANG RJES GNANG SOGS

@057A *, ,TE SMAN 'DAM LAS GRUB PA'I GUR MGON MI TSAD TZAM, LHA

DANG LAM ZAB BRGYUD PA RKANG GANG TZAM KHYAD PAR RJE NYID KYI SKU
'DRA MI TSAD CHUNG PHYOGS TZAM BYON GTZANG ZHING RAB GNAS KYI

TZAM GNYIS BYUNG BA, PHYIS MKHAN CHEN RGYAL RTZE BA BYAMS PA NGAG

YONG ZHING DE LA KHAS GSOL BYAS NA SANGS 'GRO BA'I NGO MTSAR CAN
YE SHES SEMS DPA' DNGOS SU BZHUGS

PA'I BYIN RLABS CHE NGES, PHYI'I CHOS KHRI, LHA G-YABS, DE NANG

BDAG LA RDO LHA BZHENG BA'I RDO THONG ZHES BKA' SHOG MDZAD PA

@057B LAS NYON SGRIB PA KUN BYANG NAS, ,RDO RJE 'CHANG DBANG MYUR
GRUB SHOG ,CES SMON LAM 'DEBS PA GNANG ZHING SA PHYOGS GANG DU
PHEBS PA'AM BZHUGS KYANG RUNG 'BYUNG PO MI MA YIN MTHU BO CHE
MTHA' DAG SROG SNYING MDONG GSOL DU PHUL NAS

BKA' BZHIN BSGRUB, DGON PA SHAR SPUG TU NGAG DBANG LHA MO DBYANGS
CAN MA'I LJAGS BSNYEN MDZAD PA'I TSE ME TOG DKAR PO'I CHAR BAB PA
DANG NYE SKOR DU BRDUNG MKHAN MED KYANG PI WANG GI SGRA SNYAN PO
GSAN ZHING MTHAR ZHAL MNGON SUM DU BSTAN

NAS LUNG BSTAN KYANG THOB, SPYIR RIG PA'I GNAS LNGA DANG BYE BAG
SNYAN NGAG LA THOGS PA MED PA'I RNAM DPYOD NI SLOB DPON BSTEN NAS
YUN DU SBYANGS KYANG SKAM SKAM KHRIG CHAGS SHIG LAS YONG DKA' BAR
THAGS RTZOM GANG MDZAD SNYAN NGAG TU

'GRO BA'I BLO GROS KYI SPOBS PA NANG NAS RDOL BAR MNGON, THUB
BSTAN DGE 'PHEL DU BZHUGS PA'I DUS RDO RJE 'CHANG KUN SPANGS CHOS
RJE'I RNAM THAR THUGS RTZOM GNANG BA'I SBYAR BYANG DU SPYIR DAM
PA 'DI'I RNAM THAR MTHA' DAG NI SO SO SKYE BO'I SPYOD

YUL MA YIN PAR GONG DU BRJOD PA DGAGS 'GRUB PA DANG KHYAD PAR RJE

MKHAS PA DANG GRUB PA'I DBANG PHYUG DU MA BZHUGS PA RNAMS KYIS

@058A *, ,'ONG NGAM SNYAM SGUG SDOD YUN RING BO'I NGANG DU GNAS
KYANG GRUB PAR MA THOS BA'I MTSAMS SU YE SHES KYI MKHA' 'GRO
RNAMS KYIS CUNG ZAD BSKUL BA'I MTSAN LTAS KYANG 'DUG CING GSUNG
NGAG RIN PO CHE'I BLA MA BRGYUD PA'I

RNAM THAR GYI KHA SKONG DANG, SKAL BA DANG LDAN PA'I GANG ZAG DAG
GI RGYUD LA YE SHES KYI BYIN RLABS 'JUG PA'I MTSAMS SBYOR DU ZHAS
BYUNG BA'I NGO MTSAR BA'I LTAS NI GSUNG RTZOM PHYAG BRIS MA LAS,
ZLA BA DANG PA LA SKYES PHO MO MANG PO TSOGS TE SGRON ME

KHUR NAS RDO RING KUN SPANGS PA'I GRA PA RNAMS GAR SONG 'TSOL BA
YIN ZER NAS KHO BO'I MDUN PHYOGS SU YAD YUD MANG PO BYED PA LA,
LAN DU RJE'I GRA PA 'DI DANG 'DI ZHES BYA BA MANG PO YOD NGA YANG
YIN BYAS PAS 'O NA RNAM THAR BSHAD RGYU

YOD DAM ZER BA LA MED BA SNYAM BYAD CING SHIN TU NGO GNONG BA
ZHIG LA GNYID SAD BYUNG NAS SEMS MI BDE BA SNYAM BYED PA 'GA'
BYUNG, DE RJES KYI ZLA BA PHYI MA'I NANG DU NUB CIG RMI LAM DU
BUD MED SNUM BAG CAN MANG PO BRAG STENG ZHIG NA TSOGS

KHU DIR DIR 'DUG PA LA LTAR PHYIN PAS DE RNAMS THAMS CAD YI GE
'BA' ZHIG 'DRI ZHING KHA MI 'CHAM PA'I ZI RE BA BYED PA LA DON
GANG YIN LABS PAS, BUD MED RGAN MO BYAD DMAR CHAM ME BA SO 'JER
BA ZHIG NA RE, NGED RNAMS KHYED KYI BLA MA'I

RNAM THAR RTZOM PA YIN ZER, KHYED RNAMS LA RGYUS YOD DAM BYAS PAS
PO TI CHEN PO ZHIG 'DUG PA LA MJUB MO BTZUGS NAS 'DI PHAG MO GRU
PA'I RNAM THAR PO TI YIN 'DI'I NANG 'DRI BA YIN ZER, KHYED RNAMS
GNAS YIN BYAS PAS NGA NI SLOB

@058B DPON LA BA PA'I DUS KYI LA BA'I DUM BU ZA MKHAN GYI MKHA'
'GRO'I GTZO MO PADMA'I DRA BA CAN YIN, GZHAN GZHON NU ZHIG LA
MDZUB MO BSTAD NAS 'DI SENG GE'I DRA BA CAN YIN, GZHAN 'DI RNAMS
PHYOGS BCU NAS 'DUS PAR 'DUG ZER DE RJES

GNYID SAD BSAMS PAR RJE BLA MA PHAG MO GRU PA'I RNAM SPRUL YIN PA
NI NGES PA CAN DU 'DUG SNYAM PA BYUNG, DE NAS ZHAG 'GA' SONG BA
NA NUB GSUM BSTUD NAS RMI LAM DU 'DRE MNAN GYI RNAM PA YANG YANG
DU 'ONG BA ZHIG BYUNG PAS 'DI 'DRA'I RIGS NE GU

BA RNAMS RLUNG DBU MAR 'JUG KHA MA'I 'OD GSAL GYI RTAGS SU BYED,
MGON PO'I RGYUD DUR KHROD NAG PO NAS GRIB GNON LTA BUR 'ONG BA
DANG ZHES CHOS SKYONG GI RTAGS SU'ANG BSHAD, GANG LTAR DGE SBYOR
DU BSRANGS PA DRAG SNYAM PA BYAS PAS

NUB BZHI PA'I RMI LAM DU SNGAR GYI BUD MANG DE BYUNG NAS LAG TU
SNAG TSA THOD PA GANG DANG LCAGS SMYUG CIG GTAD BYUNG NAS DED
RNAMS KYIS GANG LABS KYANG MI GO BAR 'DUG, MI GZHAN GYI BLA MA'I
GRA PAS BLA MA'I RNAM THAR 'CHOS KYI 'DUG ZER BA'I

'PHRO LA GNYID SAD BYUNG BAS KHA SANG NAS KYI LTAS THAMS CAD 'DER
'DUG PAS DA SANG RANG NAS, RJE'I RNAM THAR RTZOM DGOS SNYAM PA
BYAS NAM LANGS DGE SBYOR GRUB NAS GNYID ZIR TZAM BYUNG BA'I RMI
LAM DU CHOS KHRI ZHIG GI STENG NAS BANDE GZHON NU

ZHIG GIS SKYES RABS DPAG BSAM 'KHRI SHING SGROG GIN 'DUG PA NYAN
MKHAN YIN ZER BUD MED GZHON NU MTSOR LO MANG PO GLU LEN RKANG BRO
BYED KYIN 'DUG PA RMIS, SANG DE NAS 'GO BTZUGS NAS BRTZAMS PAS MA
GRUB BAR LA RJE BLA MA LAN GSUM RMIS,

RANG GI SROL LA LHA MO GSANG SGRUB RJES GNANG 'DI RDOG BA'I BSTAN
BA ZIN NGES SHIG LA BYED PA'I LUGS YIN GSUNGS

NAS GSANG SGRUB KYI RJES GNANG CHO GA SHIN TU RGYAS PA'I SGO NAS

KYI LTAS BYUNG BA'I RJES NUB MANG PO'I BAR DU SDIG PA DAG PA'I
RMIS

GSUNGS PA SPANG RTOGS MTHON POR SLEBS PA'I RIGS TSOR BLA MAR SRI
